## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CreateFile: Test Starts
    CreateFile --> ValidateHeaders: File Created
    ValidateHeaders --> CheckMatch: Parse Headers
    CheckMatch --> CheckExtraColumns: Headers Compared
    CheckExtraColumns --> Success: Match Found
    CheckExtraColumns --> Failure: No Match
    Success --> [*]: Return true
    Failure --> [*]: Return false
```
